<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_ae645d75-a991-4f9c-bce5-9007bcaa87ed'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer4312737751311848841">Ty Benson is tall, dark, delicious – and done with women. As the singer for the iconic rock band Raincheck, Ty is sick of women chasing after him.   <span id="freeText4312737751311848841" style="display:none">Ty Benson is tall, dark, delicious – and done with women. As the singer for the iconic rock band Raincheck, Ty is sick of women chasing after him. He’s sworn off relationships, enjoying the simplicity that celibacy brings. Until he meets Liv Madison. She’s completely – and maddeningly - uninterested in him. And it’s seriously turning him on. Stuck together on Raincheck’s Summer Tour, Ty is trying to stay away from her. But it’s getting harder every day.<br /><br />Liv Madison just wants to work on her Master’s thesis and have some fun this summer. Which is the exact reason she’s tagging along as her best friend Gabe performs on Raincheck’s tour. Ty Benson, however, seems to have other plans for her. As annoying as he is gorgeous, Ty just won’t leave her alone. And it’s affecting her relationship with Gabe - in a completely unexpected way.<br /><br />Can Ty convince Liv to give him a chance? Or will her friendship with Gabe turn into so much more?</span>
  <a data-text-id="4312737751311848841" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25765518-doris?shelf=rock-star-romance">rock-star-romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2077722841" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12715592159760909069">Can a friend’s brother actually live with you and love you without anything else going on? Friendships can be hard to come by so Liv didn’t want to do anything to mess up their special bond. Going out on tour with Gabe’s band for a few months sounded like so much fun; spending time with your friends and listening to some great music. The headlining band, Raincheck, was led by a very good looking guy named Ty. Ty had been through a lot and wanted nothing to do with this girl who surprised him in </span>
  <span id="freeText12715592159760909069" style="display:none">Can a friend’s brother actually live with you and love you without anything else going on? Friendships can be hard to come by so Liv didn’t want to do anything to mess up their special bond. Going out on tour with Gabe’s band for a few months sounded like so much fun; spending time with your friends and listening to some great music. The headlining band, Raincheck, was led by a very good looking guy named Ty. Ty had been through a lot and wanted nothing to do with this girl who surprised him in his bunk on the bus. All Liv was doing when confronted with a very angry Ty was taking a nap in Gabe’s bunk before they left for the tour. The only problem was Liv had picked the wrong bus to get on in the first place.<br /><br /> Between Gabe, Ty and Liv this story kept me engrossed over what and how was this going to work out for them especially since it was Ty who was giving Gabe’s band a break by claiming a spot on Raincheck’s tour? This author wasn’t afraid to mess with my heart because it was broken and put back together so many times that it was exhausting. She also made me hold out for hope and giving me the HEA I was looking for.<br /><br />I received this book as an ARC from NetGalley for a freely given and honest review.<br /></span>

  <span id="freeText1411815260867600297" style="display:none">This is an engaging and very fun read for those who enjoy adult romances, especially intriguing love triangles and snappy dialogue. I liked the "will-she, won't-she" thread throughout. Set in the whirlwind of a rock tour, Liv begins to fall in love with the one person on the tour that she doesn't like - at least not at first. But her feelings for Raincheck's lead singer Ty Benson aren't the only problem for her. Her best friend Gabe, with whom she's engaged in some mild subterfuge, has begun developing feelings of his own for her. Will Liv choose the steady and handsome Gabe or the sexy, deceptively tough Ty? It's definitely worth your while if you're a romance buff - and be prepared for an emotional rollercoaster that won't step until you get to the end! </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

<span id="freeTextContainer7356678897689632143">A fun, sexy,and yes, at times, maddening read. The characters were fun and flirty and real; the sex was, well, sexy; yet some of the indecision and flip-flopping was maddening. Their angst drew me in and I wanted to reach into the pages and shake them. ;) I can understand emotions getting the best of us and sometimes taking away our rational thought. Sweet ending that gave me more to think on with anticipation for stories with the secondary characters. </span>

          </span>

<div id="review_2251831173" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2251831173" />
    <a title="Marieke ~ Marieke&#39;s Books" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14546438-marieke-marieke-s-books"><img alt="Marieke ~ Marieke&#39;s Books" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1476543613p2/14546438.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2251831173?book_show_action=true">Jan 11, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Marieke ~ Marieke&#39;s Books" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Marieke ~ Marieke&#39;s Books" href="/user/show/14546438-marieke-marieke-s-books">Marieke ~ Marieke&#39;s Books</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14546438-marieke-marieke-s-books?shelf=double-pov">double-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14546438-marieke-marieke-s-books?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14546438-marieke-marieke-s-books?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14546438-marieke-marieke-s-books?shelf=rockstar">rockstar</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2251831173" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4363228445666879918">Rockstars, young people on the road, miscommunications; all ingredients for a good story. <i>Raincheck</i> by Marlo Lanz has all those things, and more. From what I can see, this is the author’s debut book, and I’m pleasantly surprised; I’ve enjoyed reading the story of Ty and Liv.<br/><blockquote>
  <i>“I hated the way Ty made me feel. It was like a whirlwind of emotions when we were together. He could drive me from furious to astonished in mere seconds. And it was maddening.”</i>
</blockquote><br/>Liv is a serious student who’s working on he</span>
  <span id="freeText4363228445666879918" style="display:none">Rockstars, young people on the road, miscommunications; all ingredients for a good story. <i>Raincheck</i> by Marlo Lanz has all those things, and more. From what I can see, this is the author’s debut book, and I’m pleasantly surprised; I’ve enjoyed reading the story of Ty and Liv.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I hated the way Ty made me feel. It was like a whirlwind of emotions when we were together. He could drive me from furious to astonished in mere seconds. And it was maddening.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Liv is a serious student who’s working on her master thesis. As a summer vacation she decides to join her dear friend and roommate Gabe while he tours with Raincheck, one of the hottest bands of the moment. To protect her from ‘wild rockstars’, she and Gabe pretend to be in a committed relationship, which isn’t that hard since they know each other so well. Getting to know the real Ty, not the version portrait by the tabloids, makes Liv question their decision.<br /><br />After the fallout with his ex-fiancé Ty isn’t interested in women anymore. Well, he had his wild period after the breakup, but now he’s trying to be good, no more booze, no more hookups with too eager groupies. Just enjoying his music and touring with his band. The ‘girlfriend’ from a guy of one of the supporting acts makes him feel things he shouldn’t feel, but he can’t stay away from her.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“She wanted me to kiss her. I could feel it. I bit the inside of my lip, warring inside, knowing this was wrong. Knowing that I should walk away before things went too far.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><i>Raincheck</i> is a rockstar romance, but beside the music also Liv's study plays an important role. The story is told in a double POV, and given what happens throughout the book I’m glad the author has written it this way. <i>Raincheck</i> has its funny moments, but there’s enough angst and moments you want to shake some sense into the characters. Are there clichés? Yes, there are, but since this is a debut book and I like the author’s writing-style, I don’t mind that much.<br /><br />Some of Liv and Ty’s actions made me shake my head, but I can ‘forgive’ them for some of those. They meet under not so normal circumstances, which makes it hard to get to know each other. Add to that Liv’s fake relationship with her best friend, a mean ex-fiancé and miscommunication and you have a disaster in the making. Peeps, please… Talk to each other, don’t assume things, don’t listen to meddling people! But then again, Liv and Ty are young, and young people make mistakes (and hopefully learn from them). I love Ty and Liv as a couple, they just make sense.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“There was something between us right from the start. Something that I’ve never felt with anyone before. Liv, you have my heart and my love. Always.” “You’re my other half.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.mariekesbooks.com">www.mariekesbooks.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="4363228445666879918" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <a title="A.BookNerd.Bookseller&amp;Bibliophile.Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="A.BookNerd.Bookseller&amp;Bibliophile.Blog" href="/user/show/67999632-a-booknerd-bookseller-bibliophile-blog">A.BookNerd.Bookseller&amp;Bibliophile.Blog</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2249741362" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13848536423428639794">So I’ve read my fair share of rockstar romances over the past year or so. It tends to be my go-to type of romance book. Raincheck is an entertaining read. It wasn’t the best one I’ve read but I definitely wanted to keep reading to find out what happened with Ty and Liv. The characters are well written and once you get to know him you can’t help but fall in love with Ty. I don’t want to give anything away so I’ll be vague in stating that some of the anger went on longer than it needed to. Also Ga</span>
  <span id="freeText13848536423428639794" style="display:none">So I’ve read my fair share of rockstar romances over the past year or so. It tends to be my go-to type of romance book. Raincheck is an entertaining read. It wasn’t the best one I’ve read but I definitely wanted to keep reading to find out what happened with Ty and Liv. The characters are well written and once you get to know him you can’t help but fall in love with Ty. I don’t want to give anything away so I’ll be vague in stating that some of the anger went on longer than it needed to. Also Gabe’s nickname for Liv annoyed me. But apart from that I recommend reading Raincheck especially if you are a rockstar romance fan. <br /><br />Reviewed by: Alexis B.</span>

<div id="review_2090707289" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2090707289" />
    <a title="Emma" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69664754-emma"><img alt="Emma" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1592212634p2/69664754.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2090707289?book_show_action=true">Aug 22, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emma" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emma" href="/user/show/69664754-emma">Emma</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2090707289" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16115391308520315441">*1.5 stars<br/><br/>This contains spoilers but I wouldn't ever recommend this book for enjoyment purposes so just read this and enjoy my rant.<br/><br/>I do <b>NOT</b> like this book! At all. For three main reasons:<br/><br/><u>The Plot</u><br/><br/>This plot is the most cliché plot I could have imagined. It was like every sort of cliché from a romantic film was spoon-fed into it. It was tacky and unbelievable I cannot understand how someone can connect with it (although I am aware and respect those people who do). This book reminded me very much o</span>
  <span id="freeText16115391308520315441" style="display:none">*1.5 stars<br /><br />This contains spoilers but I wouldn't ever recommend this book for enjoyment purposes so just read this and enjoy my rant.<br /><br />I do <b>NOT</b> like this book! At all. For three main reasons:<br /><br /><u>The Plot</u><br /><br />This plot is the most cliché plot I could have imagined. It was like every sort of cliché from a romantic film was spoon-fed into it. It was tacky and unbelievable I cannot understand how someone can connect with it (although I am aware and respect those people who do). This book reminded me very much of After which (against general consensus) I don't like however after reading this I would rate After so much higher. It was typical girl falls in love with bad boy and it really didn't work. <br /><br /><u>The Characters mainly Ty fucking Benson</u><br />For anyone to read this book and find Ty Benson any of the following: attractive, lovable, romantic I'm sorry but you may have issues. I have never met a more manipulative character in my 15 (give or take) years I have been able to read. Forget about the fact that the story jumps from Ty and Liv's first meeting where they hate each other to 3 weeks later when Ty is suddenly in love with her. Lanz I would have understood if you included the development of his love, I might have even enjoyed this book but no Sir. Ty for the most part of this book STALKS Liv. He stalks her. Red flag waving there. He doesn't leave her alone when she repeatedly makes it clear she doesn't want to talk to him. <b>HOWEVER</b> she starts to develop feelings for him because of this. What. I have bookmarked at least 30 pages in this book where Ty's actions have made me feel so very uncomfortable. He abuses his position as a musician to trap and trick Liv into falling in love with him. He lies to her yet she doesn't seem to mind. He physically corners her several times when she doesn't want to be with him and on a number of occasions grabs her which is a NO for me. <br /><br />AND THEN after all HE has done she feels bad and as though SHE treated him badly and HE lets her feel this way. This relationship is far from romantic. <br /><br />Overall I don't really like any of the character's Liv, whilst not deserving of how she is treated, is stubborn and just...stupid. The other characters are quite clearly implanted for the plot and nothing really works. <br /><br /><u>The Relationships</u><br />Everyone's in love with everyone in this book making it even more ridiculous. Reading the description of this book I was expecting a love triangle but I was disappointed. Aaahhh no. I'm so glad to be done with this book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16115391308520315441" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer13820726486429141244"><br/>Thanks to @marlo_lanz for providing me a copy of her book for an honest review! It allowed me to read outside of my comfort zone! I enjoyed and flew through it! <br/><br/>This book travels between two points of view. Ty, a handsome singer who has had his share of women. However, things get complicated when Liv doesn’t reciprocate his feelings and appears to have a relationship of her own with another membe</span>
  <span id="freeText13820726486429141244" style="display:none"><br />Thanks to @marlo_lanz for providing me a copy of her book for an honest review! It allowed me to read outside of my comfort zone! I enjoyed and flew through it! <br /><br />This book travels between two points of view. Ty, a handsome singer who has had his share of women. Despite being able to get any girl and wanting a break from women, he falls head over heels for Liv. However, things get complicated when Liv doesn’t reciprocate his feelings and appears to have a relationship of her own with another member of the tour.<br /><br />Will Liv finally see that she is the one and only for Ty, or is she content to take her relationship with her best friend to the next level? <br /><br />I enjoyed the alternating points of view and the drama that was created by this love triangle. It had me wanting to shake them and root for them at the same time.<br /><br />Romance readers are sure to enjoy this fast-paced, intense, love story! <br /><br />“If there’s someone who has your heart, don’t give up. Work it out.”</span>

<div id="review_2278710322" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2278710322" />
    <a title="Nikita" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/73156725-nikita"><img alt="Nikita" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518360604p2/73156725.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2278710322?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nikita" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nikita" href="/user/show/73156725-nikita">Nikita</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2278710322" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1812830365040798918">First things first, let's talk about the breathtaking cover of RainCheck! It is SO beautiful, that I decided to dive into Raincheck without second thoughts. I was wishing from the start, that it would live up to my expectations as the blurb sounded divine! And I happily admit that I enjoyed this rock star romance thoroughly. I couldn't put it down!<br/><br/>Meet Liv, who is doing her master in thesis and enjoys shopping & food very much!! She's tall, Hazel eyed & straightforward person. This summer, Liv g</span>
  <span id="freeText1812830365040798918" style="display:none">First things first, let's talk about the breathtaking cover of RainCheck! It is SO beautiful, that I decided to dive into Raincheck without second thoughts. I was wishing from the start, that it would live up to my expectations as the blurb sounded divine! And I happily admit that I enjoyed this rock star romance thoroughly. I couldn't put it down!<br /><br />Meet Liv, who is doing her master in thesis and enjoys shopping &amp; food very much!! She's tall, Hazel eyed &amp; straightforward person. This summer, Liv gets a chance to witness the sensational tour with band 'Raincheck' &amp; 'Diesel'.<br />Diesel is owned by her best friend &amp; roommate Gabe. He's strong built, handsome and just the ideal guy she could dream of. Not to mention great bonding with each other's families too. But the problems starts piling up when:<br />1. Liv starts finding Ty (Lead singer of Raincheck) attractive!<br />2. Gabe offers to take their friendship to the next level!<br /><br />Who would she choose?<br />This is one story that made me feel all warm and fuzzy, while being extremely sizzling hot at the same time. The love scenes between the protagonists were absolute delightful to read. The book is written in double POV, Ty's POV made me see that sometimes, how difficult live's can be for superstars, there is always a reason why a person appears to so. I LOVED the first half of the book, the thing that striked me odd in the secondary chapters was Ty's, diplomatic &amp; manipulative behavior, it didn't feel right at times as he used his money &amp; power to be around Liv even when she clearly wanted space. I wish the ending could have been a little more different...<br /><br />All in all: I'd totally recommend Raincheck for some good romance. Also, did I mention how sexy this was? Because DAMN. I can't wait to read more from this author. This was her debut novel. &lt;3</span>
  <a data-text-id="1812830365040798918" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2249396186" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2249396186" />
    <a title="Amanda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5091219-amanda"><img alt="Amanda" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2249396186?book_show_action=true">Jan 09, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amanda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amanda" href="/user/show/5091219-amanda">Amanda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2249396186" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15288450347042428077">This book is a bit of a conundrum for me. It wasn't particularly great, it was rife with cliches and excessive drama and the characters made me crazy with their immaturity and lack of communication. That being said, the author still managed to grab hold of my attention, so much so that I read this book in one sitting. I couldn't put it down. I had to know what was going to happen.<br/><br/>This is toted as a rockstar book, and while two of the main characters are rockstars, I feel that some of the other p</span>
  <span id="freeText15288450347042428077" style="display:none">This book is a bit of a conundrum for me. It wasn't particularly great, it was rife with cliches and excessive drama and the characters made me crazy with their immaturity and lack of communication. That being said, the author still managed to grab hold of my attention, so much so that I read this book in one sitting. I couldn't put it down. I had to know what was going to happen.<br /><br />This is toted as a rockstar book, and while two of the main characters are rockstars, I feel that some of the other plotlines overrode that. Liv is a grad student, tagging along with her best friend, Gabe, on his summer tour. She's hoping for a summer filled with fun, while working on her thesis on the side.<br /><br />Things start off on rocky note when Liv finds herself accidentally napping in Ty's bunk, the lead singer of Raincheck, and he freaks out. Gabe has the brilliant idea of telling everyone Liv is his girlfriend to keep Ty from kicking her off the tour. She's forbidden from coming near him again. But he keeps showing up wherever she is. Gabe turns into a raving lunatic when he realizes that things are heating up between Liv and Ty.<br /><br />There's lots of ups and downs, and the lack of communication has all the characters having breakdowns. I raged, I laughed, I swooned, I rolled my eyes. This book had me all over the place. Despite all that, I still enjoyed this book. I also enjoyed some of the secondary characters and wouldn't mind reading their stories, should the author ever decide to write them. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15288450347042428077" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Rayanne Haines" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/68769458-rayanne-haines"><img alt="Rayanne Haines" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1497979199p2/68769458.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13863889340987466274">I don’t normally read contemporary romance but I read this book after hearing about it from a friend. I really enjoyed it! I loved the witty dialogue between Liv and Ty, and authentic friendship between Liv and Gabe. The characters were fun, the sex was sexy, and the indecision heartfelt and believable. I’m looking forward to book two! 4.5 stars<br/></span>

<div id="review_2221400120" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2221400120" />
    <a title="Jennifer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7060902-jennifer"><img alt="Jennifer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1500280686p2/7060902.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2221400120?book_show_action=true">Dec 21, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer" href="/user/show/7060902-jennifer">Jennifer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7060902-jennifer?shelf=arc-books-completed">arc-books-completed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7060902-jennifer?shelf=books-ive-reviewed">books-ive-reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2221400120" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7033177442854650356">This book is about a girl and a rocker.  Sounds like many other books, right?  Not Really.  This book takes the typical rocker romance and throws in a best friend turned fake boyfriend, a tour bus, and some crazy misunderstandings to keep you thinking the entire time you are reading.  Right from the beginning I was wondering what the heck was going to happen next.  No matter the feelings of those involved, it looked hopeless.  Then things would change, and they would look even more hopeless.  I </span>
  <span id="freeText7033177442854650356" style="display:none">This book is about a girl and a rocker.  Sounds like many other books, right?  Not Really.  This book takes the typical rocker romance and throws in a best friend turned fake boyfriend, a tour bus, and some crazy misunderstandings to keep you thinking the entire time you are reading.  Right from the beginning I was wondering what the heck was going to happen next.  No matter the feelings of those involved, it looked hopeless.  Then things would change, and they would look even more hopeless.  I was beginning to think things would never work out.  But this is a romance, and what is a romance without a HEA, right? <br />Ty is a not so typical rocker.  He is genuinely a good guy, with a crappy past.  He is so confused about what he wants.  He doesn't know why Liv affects him the way he does.  He doesn't understand why he feels compelled to be around her (stalker, much?  Just kidding, kind of.)  But the more he is around her, the more he likes what he sees. <br />Liv is a woman who knows what she wants, and isn't afraid to work for it.  But she has no luck with guys.  After a less than impressive first meeting with Ty, and then the whole boyfriend that isn't really a boyfriend fiasco, it doesn't seem to be getting any better. <br />This book seems to be one comedic error after another.  I couldn't help but laugh, even though at the same time I felt bad for Liv and Ty. <br />This is the first book written by Marlo Lanz, which I totally enjoyed.  I'm looking forward to seeing what else this fantastic new author comes out with.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7033177442854650356" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

If they were freshman in college, I would buy their immaturity but to make it this far into their education in this field it just doesn't fit. <br/><br/>Ty was so incredibly manipulative throughout the book that I find it hard to believe that anyone could love him.   <span id="freeText9003380558451511685" style="display:none">I found all the characters involved to be incredibly immature despite two beginning PhD programs in psychology. If they were freshman in college, I would buy their immaturity but to make it this far into their education in this field it just doesn't fit. <br /><br />Ty was so incredibly manipulative throughout the book that I find it hard to believe that anyone could love him. He manipulated everything: Gabe, Liv, Piper, Liv's education, Liv's future and even risked the future of his band (how he can be so popular and still work an on the campus teaching assistant job makes no sense to me). He played with people's lives and didn't care who he hurt as long as he got what he wanted. And in the end he did. The author shows us if you want something bad enough just manipulate everything until you get it. <br /><br />By the way this book is $6.99 on Amazon for a digital version. There's no way I would ever consider paying that much for a digital book unless it was absolutely amazing. Save your money...this isn't worth it.<br /><br />** ARC received from Netgalley ** </span>

  <span id="freeText2055685224077019454" style="display:none">I loved the relationship triangle between Ty, Liv and Gabe and for me it read as more a YA romance, setting up a good girl with a bad boy and a confused best friend. <div id="review_2251352797" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2251352797" />
    <a title="Jackie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7088767-jackie"><img alt="Jackie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595036104p2/7088767.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2251352797?book_show_action=true">Jan 30, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jackie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jackie" href="/user/show/7088767-jackie">Jackie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2251352797" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9100724828541394670">This summer is supposed to be the greatest experience ever for Liv. Before it even starts she pisses off one of the guys in the band heading the tour. With one little fib to keep her on the tour begins a complicated lie. Pretending to date her best friend is the only way to stay on the tour. That and avoiding Ty Benson.<br/><br/>Ty realizes he should avoid Liv. They definitely got off on the wrong foot, not to mention she is dating one of the guys from their opening act. He knows all this but there is jus</span>
  <span id="freeText9100724828541394670" style="display:none">This summer is supposed to be the greatest experience ever for Liv. Before it even starts she pisses off one of the guys in the band heading the tour. With one little fib to keep her on the tour begins a complicated lie. Pretending to date her best friend is the only way to stay on the tour. That and avoiding Ty Benson.<br /><br />Ty realizes he should avoid Liv. They definitely got off on the wrong foot, not to mention she is dating one of the guys from their opening act. He knows all this but there is just something about her. He begins following her to the coffee shops she goes to on the breaks between shows.<br /><br />As Ty and Liv become closer, they can’t fight the attraction. Unfortunately, because of Liv’s complicated relationship with her best friend she is torn about what to do. Should she give a relationship with her best friend a real try or should she follow the pull that comes with Ty. In the end, who will find a way to be together? Or will love fall to the wayside. It was supposed to be the greatest experience after all.<br /><br />This was a really great book. I enjoyed the love triangle and the angst. However, I’d say the only complaint I would have would be that sometimes it got to be a bit much. Liv became too consumed with being stubborn and Ty became a bit too manipulative to get his way. In the end certain aspects of that were ignored when in reality they would have been more important some of the other aspects that made Liv mad. The side characters of Piper, Gabe and Laina were quite enjoyable. Especially, Laina, Liv’s other best friend and Gabe’s sister. She cut to the chase when Liv and Ty were dancing around each other. Overall, it was an enjoyable read. I’d recommend this for anyone looking for an angsty rock and roll romance. I look forward to the next book that I hope will be Gabe’s!</span>

<div id="review_2319590564" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2319590564" />
    <a title="Aimee Ann" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/71270194-aimee-ann"><img alt="Aimee Ann" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2319590564?book_show_action=true">Mar 07, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aimee Ann" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aimee Ann" href="/user/show/71270194-aimee-ann">Aimee Ann</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2319590564" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3221934355613094213">Raincheck is an incredible, moving and enticing romance novel that will surely entertain its readers for hours on end. Raincheck is a book I love and the type of romance I love to read; I loved Raincheck as it features my guilty pleasure… love triangles! Now, I now that some readers do not like love triangles, and I too was the same for a long time, however, Marlo Lanz’s love triangle is different than most and will charm her readers for many hours.<br/><br/>Raincheck follows the protagonist of the novel,</span>
  <span id="freeText3221934355613094213" style="display:none">Raincheck is an incredible, moving and enticing romance novel that will surely entertain its readers for hours on end. Raincheck is a book I love and the type of romance I love to read; I loved Raincheck as it features my guilty pleasure… love triangles! Now, I now that some readers do not like love triangles, and I too was the same for a long time, however, Marlo Lanz’s love triangle is different than most and will charm her readers for many hours.<br /><br />Raincheck follows the protagonist of the novel, Liv Madison as she decides to spend her summer by joining her best friend Gabe, on tour with his band but her summer gets off to a rocky start when she finds herself in an argument with one of the lead guys. Fearful that she will be kicked off the trip, she decides to enlist the help of her best friend and ask him to pretend to be her boyfriend.<br /><br />Liv Madison is a pro at pretending to date her best friend however the lines are soon blurred when Ty Benson, the star of Raincheck who has decided that he will never get in a relationship again, starts to fall for Liv. He knows that Liv is not single but he can’t help but feel attracted to her and a pull to her and what he does not know is that Liv feels the same way too. Liv and Ty will soon become more and more attracted to each other however feelings have started to grow between Gabe and Liv also. Liv will have to make a choice whether to start a relationship with Ty or pursue a relationship with Gabe. Who will she choose? You will have to read this phenomenal book to find out!<br /><br />The story of Raincheck can only be described as a guilty pleasure that is a delight to read. I personally love books such as this one because they make for adorable, quick and entertaining reads that are perfect for those that live a busy life. The story is one that will captivate its readers and evoke many feelings in them, and this is thanks to the emotive language courtesy of the wonderful Marlo Lanz.<br /><br />Marlo Lanz is an incredible woman who clearly has a phenomenal talent at grasping her reader’s attention and keeping them entertained for many hours on end. As I read Lanz’s book I felt as if she had a spell on me because I could not put her book down! When I did have to put Raincheck down, I felt myself drawn to it and wanted to be reunited with the story once again. When a reader feels this it shows that not only the author is a talented wordsmith but also a fantastic storyteller.<br /><br />As Marlo Lanz is a remarkable woman who knows how to write romantic fiction in the most stellar of ways, I have no choice but to award this brilliant book a dazzling five stars! So please, if you are a reader who is looking to get lost in an emotive romance then Raincheck is for you!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3221934355613094213" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2282135795?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nela" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nela" href="/user/show/24157456-nela">Nela</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24157456-nela?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2282135795" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14527724270321632621">I finished reading a day ago and the characters are still on my mind. That's how I know that Raincheck is a good book. <br/><br/>The author, Marlo Lanz, sent me a free copy in exchange for an honest review. The romance is about Liv, a witty masters student who I would best describe as the girl next door. She is forced to choose between Gabe, her best friend, and Ty, the guy she just met. Both men are sexy. Gabe is sweet, caring, and safe. Ty is a rockstar, moody, womanizing, dangerous. But, there is more </span>
  <span id="freeText14527724270321632621" style="display:none">I finished reading a day ago and the characters are still on my mind. That's how I know that Raincheck is a good book. <br /><br />The author, Marlo Lanz, sent me a free copy in exchange for an honest review. The romance is about Liv, a witty masters student who I would best describe as the girl next door. She is forced to choose between Gabe, her best friend, and Ty, the guy she just met. Both men are sexy. Gabe is sweet, caring, and safe. Ty is a rockstar, moody, womanizing, dangerous. But, there is more to him than meets the eye. The more Liv gets to know him, the less obvious her choice becomes. <br /><br />I loved the "will she, won't she" aspect of this story. It was exciting and maddening at the same time. I kept coming back for more. As a Canadian, I was happy to see the dialect and BC setting. I enjoyed Marlo's writing style. Reading the story from both Liv and Ty's perspectives was perfectly descriptive. I wasn't confused about the characters and the plot. All loose ends were nicely tied together. <br /><br />The sex scenes were raw and definately steamy but mostly involved foreplay. Liv said that she would go "all the way" with the man that she loved. However, we don't see that when she makes her choice in the end. I would have liked to see just one more love scene. <br /><br />Overall, a fun and entertaining romance. 4 stars! I look forward to reading more from Marlo.</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11986295452649776902">I voluntarily reviewed an Advance Reader Copy of the book.<br/><br/>I enjoyed this book way more than I was expecting - I found myself making excuses to get out of other tasks just so that I could continue reading. Raincheck was engaging from the very beginning - Liv is a very likable character and relatable character and clues as to Gabe's feelings for her are laid from the start, leading to an angsty and entertaining love triangle of sorts. The introduction of Ty is funny and his reaction to her is ende</span>
  <span id="freeText11986295452649776902" style="display:none">I voluntarily reviewed an Advance Reader Copy of the book.<br /><br />I enjoyed this book way more than I was expecting - I found myself making excuses to get out of other tasks just so that I could continue reading. Raincheck was engaging from the very beginning - Liv is a very likable character and relatable character and clues as to Gabe's feelings for her are laid from the start, leading to an angsty and entertaining love triangle of sorts. The introduction of Ty is funny and his reaction to her is endearing, while Liv's perception of both men and their feelings and intent is adorably oblivious. Not only does the book feature a love triangle, it has a fake relationship element as well - though I felt that that aspect was held on to for a bit too long. The pacing was fantastic (not too fast and not too slow) until the last 30 - 40% and then it really did drag which changed my rating. It got to the point where I didn't understand the point of dragging out the book and I found myself rushing through it. I still really enjoyed the story and see great potential for a series here - Marlo Lane is a talented writer and I loved her story telling style. 3.5 out of 5 wine glasses. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11986295452649776902" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer5321460353654960366">Raincheck by Marlo Lanz is a fun little romp of a book about the rock and roll industry, and all of the crazy relationships that are part of that industry. From Liv who just wants to tour with her friend Gabe's band Raincheck, to Ty, who is downright cute and sexy, this is a mashup of fun characters and enough sexual tension to drown in. While the characters may come across as a little immature, they are still interesting, if only for their interactions with each other, and how manipulative they</span>
  <span id="freeText5321460353654960366" style="display:none">Raincheck by Marlo Lanz is a fun little romp of a book about the rock and roll industry, and all of the crazy relationships that are part of that industry. From Liv who just wants to tour with her friend Gabe's band Raincheck, to Ty, who is downright cute and sexy, this is a mashup of fun characters and enough sexual tension to drown in. While the characters may come across as a little immature, they are still interesting, if only for their interactions with each other, and how manipulative they can be. Ty is probably the worst of the manipulators, but ultimately Gabe is too, to some degree. With these kind of complications, Liv doesn't know what to do, or who to fall for. Overall, a fun book, that takes a less than serious look at rock and roll, relationships, and the ties that bind. A light read for a fun diversion.</span>

Romance novels are not something I read that often, so I was pleased that this one was definitely a welcome break from thrillers and horror.<br/><br/>The steamy love triangle in this flirty romance, will have readers asking the questions: “will they, wont they?” and “who will she choose?” many times throughout the story.   <span id="freeText7516463874366357406" style="display:none">Marlo Lanz seems set to become well established as a romance author, if Raincheck is anything to go by. It is competently written, with a compelling plot, and 3-dimensional characters. Romance novels are not something I read that often, so I was pleased that this one was definitely a welcome break from thrillers and horror.<br /><br />The steamy love triangle in this flirty romance, will have readers asking the questions: “will they, wont they?” and “who will she choose?” many times throughout the story. Liv is torn between two men, and she is stuck with them both in the confines of a tour bus. As you can imagine, tensions are high and they sometimes bubble over. Will Liv choose the manipulative, yet seductive Ty, or the more reliable, and handsome Gabe? You will have to read to the final pages to find out.<br /><br /></span>

    <a title="Luxurious Literature" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/74338326-luxurious-literature"><img alt="Luxurious Literature" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1532679946p2/74338326.jpg" /></a>

  <span id="freeText11134222224936224237" style="display:none">Those with a fondness for romance novels with a little bit of extra spice, will certainly fall for Raincheck by Marlo Lanz. This adult novel has plenty to keep the romance aficionados interested and engaged right up to the last page. The writing was decent and the pacing was spot on, with plenty of plot twists and tension that made it quite the page turner. The book focuses on a tour of the band Raincheck, fronted by the charismatic ladies man, Ty. He finds his head turned when Liv board the tour bus with her friend Gabe, a member of the supporting band. What follows in an intense and racy love story that will keep you guessing until the final pages. </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('xZ5EVwXtZyqL2TlizHVKaWmmWXiDf0xhwL/8xeU7znO12edd10N095V0M2p+rqTrYyhf8EmjK3hGAv3beQbASQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ep2TEYSicMvb1DaO39ZlOi5ir4dnx2VnhPhCicy/Y2gK2jAbVgxjFsV5PIZtDYu4JOypD60bAn4CRUOXUIJtUg==')})
  }
